ru/printer/printer.html:1138:function filteredProducts() {
ru/printer/printer.html:1139:  const query = searchInput.value.trim().toLowerCase();
ru/printer/printer.html:1140:  return products.filter((item) => {
ru/printer/printer.html:1141:    const matchesFilter = activeFilter === 'all' || item.filters.includes(activeFilter);

ru/printer/printer.html:1143:    const matchesQuery = !query || haystack.includes(query);
ru/printer/printer.html:1144:    return matchesFilter && matchesQuery;

ru/printer/printer.html:1152:  grid.hidden = data.length === 0;

ru/cpu/cpu.html:1292:function filteredProducts() {

ru/cooler/cooler.html:821:    <div class="section-head">
ru/cooler/cooler.html:822:      <div>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:823:        <span class="kicker">Выбор</span>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:825:        <p>These guidelines are adapted from the structure and descriptive content of the source category. They help filter out unsuitable models before you compare exact part numbers.</p>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:826:      </div>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:827:    </div>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:829:    <div class="guide-grid">
ru/cooler/cooler.html:830:      <article class="guide-card">
ru/cooler/cooler.html:831:        <h3>Core selection points</h3>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:833:          <li>Dissipated power should meet or exceed the CPU TDP, ideally with a practical margin.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:834:          <li>Socket support must match the exact Intel or AMD platform you are building around.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:835:          <li>Large towers and radiators should always be checked against the free space inside the case.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:836:          <li>For quieter systems, larger fan diameters with moderate RPM are usually easier to live with.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:838:      </article>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:840:      <article class="guide-card">
ru/cooler/cooler.html:841:        <h3>Materials and mechanics</h3>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:843:          <li>Radiators typically use aluminum, copper or hybrid combinations, with copper offering stronger heat transfer at a higher cost.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:844:          <li>Bearing type affects lifetime and acoustics, and the category includes several common solutions used in modern fans.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:845:          <li>If precise speed control matters, PWM support is worth prioritizing.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:846:          <li>For case fans, lighting type and connector format should be checked before purchase.</li>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:848:      </article>
ru/cooler/cooler.html:849:    </div>
